<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Read my review on Access San Fernando 24 hour vet to better understand one of the reasons why VCA Chatsworth is so appreciated by me.  This is one Five Star reviewed place that I personally vouch for.

Without getting into too much detail in this review, I'll share that I had two visits to Access on Sunday with neither one answering what was wrong with my boy.  Monday morning, I called VCA and even though they are booked solid, after hearing about my issues with the emergency vet, they squeezed in my boy.

The emergency vet could not diagnose my boy, because they said that he was too big and too strong to handle.   At VCA, the vet tells me "he isn't resisting.  He is a sweetheart.  He doesn't like to be on his side so we didn't force him. We just let him think he was in control and he let us check his paws"..... IMAGINE THAT???  A vet and vet's office that understands how to interact with their animal client....

They found that he has redness in his paw.  No puncture wounds, but definitely something to cause extreme pain.  They drew up an exam plan:  xray; blood work; sedation; etc...  Everything I had had hoped the 24 hour place would have done a day earlier, but they didn't.

VCA took care of my baby, and as a result, took care of my emotional state.  I trust them.  I don't question treatment plans.  Costly? Worth it.  I have pet insurance and even though it will still be a good amount out of pocket, it is worth it.

After my boy was discharged today, I called the office to thank the staff and the vet for taking care of my baby.< /review>

< review>
Ill give them the benefit of the doubt here because I came in right when they opened but the pizza was... Well I would say mediocre, (literally) the mushrooms and bell peppers pretty much still raw pretty much. The pizzas taste was meh. If I were to make this at home and tried to replicate it the best I could, I would slap a piece of inflated pita bread down cover it with grease, some tomatoes from the can, so they're nice and tinny, throw the onions bell peppers mushrooms and a pound of olives on there(i like olives but I didn't order a olive pizza) and meat on there. A whole package of cheese on there and throw it in the oven for 5 minutes to make sure the raw onions where the highlight of the meal and the cheese is a little over half melted. I was in town for graduation but honestly everything I found in Humboldt county was vegan co ops vegan bakeries and cafes thank god eel river brewery was on the way home! Now that place knows how to cook! And great beers on tap!</review>

<userid>107651363527543844794<//userid><user_name>Jonas Gebhardt</user_name><Time>1488145853783</Time><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
Here's how this place works: first, choose your base - salad, rice, pita or sajj bread. After that choose your meat or go vegetarian with falafel. Then, you can add various veggies. I highly recommend their eggplant which adds some great flavor. All the ingredients are super fresh and full of tasty flavors. This is real Mediterranean food. Their food isn't very salty but really relays on the flavors of the ingredients. The manager comes around and checks that everything is fine. They are really clean and friendly - what a nice experience. They also have outdoor seating.< /review>

< Review>
I recently came across this new joint in Sunnyvale downtown. I went here more of an accident, but I am so glad that I stumbled upon this place. The people here so amicable and it feels really good to go here every time.

The joint is add what you like a Mediterranean bowl/wrap place. You pick your carbs, greens, protein, dressings and any extras toppings you might want to add, and there are a lot of toppings to chose from.

Their SHAWAFEL is a delight that everyone should definitely try out. All of their greens, toppings, and protein seem very fresh and really great treat for your taste buds. I have gotten freshly made falafels on a few occasions I have been here. They make falafels in small batches so that they can keep the freshness intact.

After any meal here, I would recommend anyone and everyone to have the Baklava on the side as a desert. It was just bliss.</Review>
